NAME
    Get-SpotifyArtistTopTracks

SYNOPSIS
    Get artist's top tracks.


SYNTAX
    Get-SpotifyArtistTopTracks [-ArtistId] <String> [-Market <String>] [<CommonParameters>]


DESCRIPTION
    Get Spotify catalog information about an artist's top tracks by country.


RELATED LINKS
    https://developer.spotify.com/documentation/web-api/reference/#/operations/get-an-artists-top-tracks

REMARKS
    To see the examples, type: "Get-Help Get-SpotifyArtistTopTracks -Examples"
    For more information, type: "Get-Help Get-SpotifyArtistTopTracks -Detailed"
    For technical information, type: "Get-Help Get-SpotifyArtistTopTracks -Full"
    For online help, type: "Get-Help Get-SpotifyArtistTopTracks -Online"
